UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat5.xyz;

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat10_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat10_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat10_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat10_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = max(u_xlat39, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    u_xlat40 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat6.xy).x;
    u_xlatb40 = u_xlat40<u_xlat6.z;
    u_xlat6.x = (u_xlatb40) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat40 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat7.xy).x;
    u_xlatb40 = u_xlat40<u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat6.y = (u_xlatb40) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;

UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(7) uniform mediump sampler2D _GhostMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
vec4 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
float u_xlat13;
uint u_xlatu13;
vec3 u_xlat14;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_17;
float u_xlat18;
vec3 u_xlat20;
float u_xlat26;
int u_xlati26;
bool u_xlatb26;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat39;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
bool u_xlatb39;
float u_xlat40;
bool u_xlatb40;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
mediump float u_xlat16_43;
float u_xlat44;
bool u_xlatb44;
float u_xlat45;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = max(u_xlat39, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat6.xy,u_xlat6.z);
    u_xlat6.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat7.xy,u_xlat7.z);
    u_xlat6.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_42 = dot(u_xlat6, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_43 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_43;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb40 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb40 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb44 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb44 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb40 = u_xlatb40 || u_xlatb44;
    u_xlat16_42 = (u_xlatb40) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_42;
    u_xlat16_43 = (-u_xlat16_15) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_43 = (-u_xlat16_43) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_15;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_43;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_15 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_43 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_43 * u_xlat16_43;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat39) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat39 = min(max(u_xlat39, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;

    u_xlat16_42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;

    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat3.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat3.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat3.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat4.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat4.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat2.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_15 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_15;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb13 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb13 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb13 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_41 = (-u_xlat16_28) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat13) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 + u_xlat16_42;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_42)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_41 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = max(u_xlat16_41, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_41 = log2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_41 = exp2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_41 = exp2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = min(u_xlat16_41, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_41) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat16_42 + 1.0;
    u_xlat13 = float(1.0) / u_xlat13;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_19 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_32.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_32.x = (-u_xlat16_32.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_32.x;
    u_xlat16_32.x = u_xlat16_32.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32.x = min(max(u_xlat16_32.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32.x = clamp(u_xlat16_32.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_6.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_32.xxx + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.x = abs(u_xlat16_6.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat39 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32.x = u_xlat39 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat39 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _Cutoff * 2.0 + u_xlat16_45;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    SV_Target0.w = min(max(SV_Target0.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_32.x = u_xlat16_32.x * u_xlat16_32.x;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_32.xxx * u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat44 = u_xlat39 * 0.125 + u_xlat40;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat40);
    u_xlat10.y = u_xlat39 + 0.125;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat44 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_32.xy = max(u_xlat10.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_32.xy = u_xlat16_32.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_32.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_32.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_41) * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat39 = min(max(u_xlat39, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat40 = (-u_xlat39) * u_xlat39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat39 + u_xlat40;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat16_42 / u_xlat39;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat40;
    u_xlat39 = min(u_xlat39, 100.0);
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat39 = min(max(u_xlat39, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = max(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_12.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_15 + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);

    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat5.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_28 = (-u_xlat5.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;

    u_xlat40 = exp2(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat40 = (-u_xlat40) + 2.0;

#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_15 * -2.0 + 3.0;

    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_15 * u_xlat16_28;

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_19) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat0.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);

    u_xlat0.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);

    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.y = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_41 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_41 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_GhostChange, _GhostChange, _GhostChange)) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat40) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat40) * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat39 = min(u_xlat39, 1.0);
    u_xlat40 = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat40 + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat40 + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat40 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat5.xy = vec2(u_xlat40) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat5.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat5.xy;
    u_xlat16_40 = texture(_ClothTex, u_xlat5.xy).x;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_40 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat39 = (-u_xlat39) + u_xlat40;

    u_xlat39 = min(max(u_xlat39, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_15 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_15;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb13 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb13 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb13 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_41 = (-u_xlat16_28) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_42);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat13) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 + u_xlat16_42;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_42)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_41 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = max(u_xlat16_41, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_41 = log2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_41 = exp2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_41 = exp2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_41 = min(u_xlat16_41, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_41) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat16_42 + 1.0;
    u_xlat13 = float(1.0) / u_xlat13;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_19 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_32.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_32.x = (-u_xlat16_32.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + u_xlat16_32.x;
    u_xlat16_32.x = u_xlat16_32.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32.x = min(max(u_xlat16_32.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32.x = clamp(u_xlat16_32.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_6.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_32.xxx + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_6.x = abs(u_xlat16_6.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat39 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32.x = u_xlat39 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat39 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _Cutoff * 2.0 + u_xlat16_45;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    SV_Target0.w = min(max(SV_Target0.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_32.x = u_xlat16_32.x * u_xlat16_32.x;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_32.xxx * u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat10.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat44 = u_xlat39 * 0.125 + u_xlat40;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat40);
    u_xlat10.y = u_xlat39 + 0.125;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat44 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_32.xy = max(u_xlat10.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_32.xy = u_xlat16_32.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_32.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_32.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_41) * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat39);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat39 = min(max(u_xlat39, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat40 = (-u_xlat39) * u_xlat39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat39 + u_xlat40;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat16_42 / u_xlat39;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat40;
    u_xlat39 = min(u_xlat39, 100.0);
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat39 = min(max(u_xlat39, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = max(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_0.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_12.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_15 + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(u_xlat16_12.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat5.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_28 = (-u_xlat5.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat40 = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat40 * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat40 = exp2(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat40 = (-u_xlat40) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_28 + u_xlat39;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_41 / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_15 + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_28 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_28 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_15;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_15 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_15 * u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_15 * u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_15;

    u_xlat39 = u_xlat16_42 / u_xlat39;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_28 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_28 + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat39 = u_xlat39 * u_xlat40;
    u_xlat39 = min(u_xlat39, 100.0);
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat18.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat18.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat18.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat8.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat18.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15);

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = max(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));

    u_xlat16_15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15);

    u_xlat16_28 = (-u_xlat5.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_41 = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat40 = log2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat40 * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat40 = exp2(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat40 = (-u_xlat40) + 2.0;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_41 * u_xlat16_28 + u_xlat39;
    u_xlat16_28 = u_xlat16_41 / u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_28 * u_xlat16_15 + (-_RimlightScale);

    u_xlat16_41 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);

    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat39) * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;

        u_xlat36 = min(max(u_xlat36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
        u_xlat36 = clamp(u_xlat36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
        u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat37;
        u_xlat16_26 = dot(_AdditionalLightsSpotDir[u_xlati24].xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuation[u_xlati24].z + _AdditionalLightsAttenuation[u_xlati24].w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
        u_xlat16_26 = min(max(u_xlat16_26, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat16_26 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
        u_xlat16_26 = min(max(u_xlat16_26, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

        u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;

    u_xlat0.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat0.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat0.xy * u_xlat16_2.xx;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_GhostMap, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_6.xyz) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    SV_Target0.w = min(max(SV_Target0.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif

    u_xlat12.x = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat24 = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);

#else

    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat12.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat10_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat10_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat10_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_26, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat10_1.xyz = texture2D(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));

    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * _Emissive;

    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = max(u_xlat36, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;

    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_14) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_39) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14;
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat10_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_14) + u_xlat10_0.xyz;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Smoothness;

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat13;
float u_xlat14;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_26;

mediump float u_xlat16_38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
float u_xlat41;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
float u_xlat43;
mediump float u_xlat16_46;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_26, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = max(u_xlat36, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_14) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_39) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14 = min(max(u_xlat16_14, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_14) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_14 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14 = min(max(u_xlat16_14, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat37 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat36 = min(max(u_xlat36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat36 = clamp(u_xlat36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = abs(u_xlat16_4.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(u_xlat16_4.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat41 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat41 = min(max(u_xlat41, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat41 = clamp(u_xlat41, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat43 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat43 = min(max(u_xlat43, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat43 = clamp(u_xlat43, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat20.x = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8.z = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + u_xlat20.x;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat8.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat20.x);
    u_xlat9.xy = u_xlat8.zx + vec2(0.125, 0.125);
    u_xlat16_16.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_16.xy = u_xlat16_16.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_16.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_42 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 + u_xlat16_42;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_42)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat8.x = (-u_xlat16_4.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat8.x * u_xlat8.x;
    u_xlat16_42 = u_xlat16_42 * u_xlat16_42;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_46 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_9 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat16_46);
    u_xlat16_10.x = u_xlat16_9.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_10.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_10.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_10.x = max(u_xlat16_10.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_10.x = log2(u_xlat16_10.x);
    u_xlat16_10.x = u_xlat16_10.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_10.x = exp2(u_xlat16_10.x);
    u_xlat16_10.x = u_xlat16_10.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xxx;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat20.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat20.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat20.x;
    u_xlat20.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat20.xxx;
    u_xlat9.xyz = (-u_xlat7.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_14);
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_42) * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat20.xyz = u_xlat20.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat20.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat20.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat5.x = (-u_xlat41) * u_xlat41 + 1.0;
    u_xlat17 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat41;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat17 * u_xlat17 + u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_39 / u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat17 = u_xlat16_2.z * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat17;
    u_xlat5.x = min(u_xlat5.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat5.xyz;

        u_xlat5.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz) + _AdditionalLightsPositionDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).xyz;
        u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
        u_xlat36 = max(u_xlat36, 6.10351563e-05);
        u_xlat37 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
        u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat37) * u_xlat5.xyz;
        u_xlat37 = float(1.0) / u_xlat36;
        u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).x + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).y;
        u_xlat36 = clamp(u_xlat36, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat37;
        u_xlat16_26 = dot(_AdditionalLightsSpotDirDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).z + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).w;
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat16_26 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_26) * _AdditionalLightsColorDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).xyz;
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
        u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_16.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    }
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat0.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat0.xy * u_xlat16_2.xx;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy + _Time.xx;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_GhostMap, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = (-u_xlat16_6.xyz) + u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(vec3(_GhostChange, _GhostChange, _GhostChange)) * u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat8.x + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _Cutoff * 2.0 + u_xlat16_38;
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz / u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat36 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat1.xy = vec2(u_xlat36) * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat10_36 = texture2D(_ClothTex, u_xlat1.xy).x;
    u_xlat1.x = _DigiBaseColor1.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat13.x = max(_DigiChange, -1.0);
    u_xlat13.x = min(u_xlat13.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x + (-_DigiBaseColor0.w);
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat13.x * u_xlat1.x + _DigiBaseColor0.w;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat10_36 + vs_TEXCOORD0.y;
    u_xlat36 = (-u_xlat1.x) + u_xlat36;
    u_xlat36 = clamp(u_xlat36, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * _DigiPow;
    u_xlat1.x = exp2(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat1.x) + 2.0;
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * _DigiBaseColor0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-_DigiBaseColor0.xyz) * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat13.xyz;
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    return;
}

{

    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;

UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat13;
float u_xlat14;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _DigiST1.zw;
    u_xlat0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _DigiST1.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(_ClothTex, u_xlat0.xy, 0.0).z;
    u_xlat4.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz * vec3(vec3(_DigiDistore, _DigiDistore, _DigiDistore));
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.200000003, 0.200000003, 0.200000003) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _ClothTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _GhostMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
float u_xlat12;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_13;
vec3 u_xlat17;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_18;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_22;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_25;
float u_xlat36;
mediump float u_xlat16_37;
float u_xlat38;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
float u_xlat41;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_1.x = max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(u_xlat16_1.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_13.x = (-u_xlat16_1.x) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_25.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_25.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_25.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_25.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_25.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_25.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_25.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat12 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat12 = max(u_xlat12, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat12) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat12) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_25.x = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_25.x = u_xlat16_25.x + u_xlat16_25.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-u_xlat16_25.xxx) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_13.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_13.x = max(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_13.x = log2(u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_13.x = exp2(u_xlat16_13.x);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_13.xxx;
    u_xlat16_39 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_39 = exp2(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_39 = min(u_xlat16_39, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_13.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat12 = float(1.0) / u_xlat12;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xyz * vec3(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_25.x = u_xlat16_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_25.x = u_xlat16_25.x * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_13.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_13.x = u_xlat16_13.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_13.x = min(max(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_13.x = clamp(u_xlat16_13.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = (-u_xlat16_1.x) + u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_13.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_18.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * u_xlat16_13.xxx + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) + (-u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_13.x = abs(u_xlat16_13.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_13.x = min(u_xlat16_13.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat36 = (-u_xlat16_13.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat36;
    u_xlat16_10.x = u_xlat36 + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _Cutoff * 2.0 + u_xlat16_10.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    SV_Target0.w = min(max(SV_Target0.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    SV_Target0.w = clamp(SV_Target0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_37 = u_xlat16_37 * u_xlat16_37;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_37) * u_xlat9.xyz + u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat36 * 0.125 + u_xlat38;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat38);
    u_xlat9.y = u_xlat36 + 0.125;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat41 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat9.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_22.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_22.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat16_18.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_37 = _SHshadow + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_37 = min(max(u_xlat16_37, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_37 = clamp(u_xlat16_37, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat36 = min(max(u_xlat36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat36 = clamp(u_xlat36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat38 = (-u_xlat36) * u_xlat36 + 1.0;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_6.x * u_xlat36;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat36 + u_xlat38;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat16_6.x / u_xlat36;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat36;
    u_xlat38 = u_xlat16_1.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat16_1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat5.x = u_xlat5.x * u_xlat5.x;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat38;
    u_xlat36 = min(u_xlat36, 100.0);
    u_xlat17.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3

#endif

    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz;

    u_xlat4.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].xy * u_xlat4.xx + u_xlat1.xy;

    u_xlat12 = inversesqrt(u_xlat12);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat12) * u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat4.xy = u_xlat4.xy / _ScreenParams.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * u_xlat4.xy;

attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;

{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
